G
Main system code
The main system code is written in Python and developed for Raspberry Pi 5 with a touch
display. The code is structured into several screens/files, each with its own functionality.
The code uses the kivy library with modern kivyMD for the user interface. The main file
is main.py, which is the entry point for the application.
G.1

class ObservableDict(dict):
29
"""A dictionary that notifies observers when it changes."""
30
def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
31
super().__init__(*args, **kwargs)
32
self._observers = []
33
34
def add_observer(self, callback):
35
"""Add an observer callback."""
36
self._observers.append(callback)
37
38
def notify_observers(self):
39
"""Notify all observers of a change."""
40
for callback in self._observers:
41
callback()
42
43
def __setitem__(self, key, value):
44
super().__setitem__(key, value)
45
self.notify_observers()
46
47
def __delitem__(self, key):
48
super().__delitem__(key)
49
self.notify_observers()
50
51

52
class GlobalState:
53

def parse_usb_tree(self, usb_devices_output):
676
"""Parse the output of usb-devices to extract device information ,
including serial numbers and only specific ports."""
677
devices = []
678
current_device = {}
679
680
# Define allowed (bus, lev, port) combinations
681
allowed_ports = {
682
("01", "02", "00"),
683
("01", "02", "01"),
684
("01", "02", "02"),
685
("01", "03", "00"),
686
("01", "03", "01"),
687
("03", "02", "00"),
688
("03", "02", "01"),
689
("03", "02", "02"),
690
("03", "03", "00"),
691
("03", "03", "01"),
692
}
693
694
for line in usb_devices_output.splitlines():
695
line = line.strip()
696
697
# Detect the start of a new device
698
if line.startswith("T:"):
699
if current_device:
700
# Only add devices with allowed (bus, lev, port)
701
key = (current_device.get("bus"), current_device.get("lev"
), current_device.get("port"))
702
if key in allowed_ports:
703
devices.append(current_device)
704
current_device = {"bus": None, "lev": None, "port": None, "
serial": None}
705
706
# Extract the bus number
707
if "Bus=" in line:
708
parts = line.split()
709
for part in parts:
710
if part.startswith("Bus="):
711
current_device["bus"] = part.split("=")[1]
712
713
# Extract the Lev value
714
if "Lev=" in line:
715
parts = line.split()
716
for part in parts:
717
if part.startswith("Lev="):
718
current_device["lev"] = part.split("=")[1]
719
720
# Extract the port number (if available)
721
if "Port=" in line:
722
parts = line.split()
723
for part in parts:
724
if part.startswith("Port="):
725
current_device["port"] = part.split("=")[1]
726
727
# Extract the serial number
728
if "SerialNumber=" in line:
729
parts = line.split("SerialNumber=")
730
if len(parts) > 1:
731
current_device["serial"] = parts[1].strip()
732
733
# Add the last device if it matches allowed ports
176
Modular Incubation and Monitoring System for Sample Storage in High-Throughput Screening
==PAGE:185==
734
key = (current_device.get("bus"), current_device.get("lev"),
current_device.get("port"))
735
if current_device and key in allowed_ports:
736
devices.append(current_device)
737
738
return devices
739

# Update the `poll_usb_devices ` method to update the connected USB devices
label
763
def poll_usb_devices(self, dt):
764
"""Periodically check for changes in USB devices and update dropdowns.
"""
765
try:
766
usb_tree = subprocess.check_output("usb-devices", shell=True,
stderr=subprocess.STDOUT).decode("utf-8")
767
768
# print(f"USB devices output: {usb_tree}")
# Debugging log
769
770
self.current_usb_devices = self.parse_usb_tree(usb_tree)
771
772
# Detect removed devices
773
removed_devices = [device for device in self.previous_usb_devices
if device not in self.current_usb_devices]
774
for device in removed_devices:
775
self.clear_device_from_dropdown(device)
776
777
# Detect added devices

class ColorOverlay(BoxLayout):

box_colors = ListProperty([[0, 0, 1, 0.2]] * 6)
# One color per box

def __init__(self, **kwargs):
53

inst.pos))

inst.size))

def _update_colors(self, *args):

def start_sensor_thread(self):
337
"""Start a thread to periodically read the SHT30 sensor and update the
label."""
338
threading.Thread(target=self.update_temperature , daemon=True).start()

def update_temperature(self):
341
sensor = SHT30Sensor()
342
failure_counts = [0] * 6
# Counter for consecutive failures for each
sensor
343
temperatures = [None] * 6
# Store temperatures for all sensors
344
humidities = [None] * 6
# Store humidities for all sensors
345
346
while True:
347
for channel in range(6):
# Iterate through the 6 sensors
348
try:
349
sensor.select_channel(channel)
# Select the TCA9548A
channel
350
temperature , humidity = sensor.read_sensor()
351
if temperature is not None and humidity is not None:
352
# Reset failure count on successful read
353
failure_counts[channel] = 0
354
temperatures[channel] = temperature
355
humidities[channel] = humidity
356
# Schedule the label update on the main thread
357
Clock.schedule_once(lambda dt, ch=channel , temp=
temperature , hum=humidity: self.update_label(ch,
temp, hum))
358
else:
359
failure_counts[channel] += 1
360
print(f"Warning: Failed to read SHT30 sensor on
channel {channel} ({failure_counts[channel]} time(
s)).")
361
if failure_counts[channel] >= 3:
362
print(f"SHT30 sensor on channel {channel} not
found. Extending update interval.")
363
except Exception as e:
364
print(f"Error reading sensor on channel {channel}: {e}")
365

Modular Incubation and Monitoring System for Sample Storage in High-Throughput Screening

def on_temperature_change(self, label, value, unit="°C"):
523
"""Callback for temperature slider."""

Modular Incubation and Monitoring System for Sample Storage in High-Throughput Screening

==PAGE:204==

0.05)

control is disabled.")

self.pid_M.setpoint = value

self.pid_R.setpoint = value

def temperature_to_color(self, temperature):
765
t = max(self.min_temperature , min(self.max_temperature , temperature))
766
norm = (t - self.min_temperature) / (self.max_temperature - self.
min_temperature)
767
if norm < 0.33:
768
r = 0
769
g = norm / 0.33
770
b = 1 - g
771
elif norm < 0.66:
772
r = (norm - 0.33) / 0.33
773
g = 1
774
b = 0
775
else:
776
r = 1
777
g = 1 - ((norm - 0.66) / 0.34)
778
b = 0
779
return [r, g, b, 0.2]
780

class SHT30Sensor:
820
def __init__(self, i2c_bus=1, address=0x44, multiplexer_address=0x70):
821
"""Initialize the SHT30 sensor with I2C communication."""
822
self.bus = SMBus(i2c_bus)
823
self.address = address
824
self.multiplexer_address = multiplexer_address
825
826
def select_channel(self, channel):
827
"""Select the TCA9548A channel."""
828
try:
829
self.bus.write_byte(self.multiplexer_address , 1 << channel)
830
except Exception as e:
831
print(f"Error selecting TCA9548A channel {channel}: {e}")
832
833
def read_sensor(self):
834
"""Read temperature and humidity from the SHT30 sensor."""
835
try:
836
# Send measurement command
837
self.bus.write_i2c_block_data(self.address , 0x2C, [0x06])
838
time.sleep(0.015)
# Wait for measurement to complete
839
840
# Read 6 bytes of data
841
data = self.bus.read_i2c_block_data(self.address , 0x00, 6)
842
843
# Convert the data
844
temperature_raw = data[0] << 8 | data[1]
845
humidity_raw = data[3] << 8 | data[4]
846
847
# Calculate temperature in Celsius
848
temperature = -45 + (175 * (temperature_raw / 65535.0))
849
850
# Calculate relative humidity in percentage
851
humidity = 100 * (humidity_raw / 65535.0)
852
853
return temperature , humidity
854
except Exception as e:
855
print(f"Error reading SHT30 sensor: {e}")
856
return None, None

Listing G.7: About screen code for the enclosure
204
Modular Incubation and Monitoring System for Sample Storage in High-Throughput Screening
==PAGE:213==
Modular Incubation and Monitoring System for Sample Storage in High-Throughput Screening
205
==PAGE:214==
This report documents the design, development, and implementation of a modular laboratory incu-
bation system featuring integrated climate control and automated modular device management. The
work covers CAD designs with technical drawings, CFD simulations, assembly guides with BOM,
electronics, and software development. The project was carried out as a Master’s thesis at the Tech-
nical University of Denmark (DTU), and aims to provide a flexible incubation platform for future
research and development in life science automation.
Technical
University of
Denmark
Produktionstorvet 427A
2800 Kgs. Lyngby
Tlf. 4525 1700
www.construct.dtu.dk
